# <a name="release-notes-for-semi-annual-enterprise-channel"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-103">半年企業通道的版本資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-103">Release notes for Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cf135-104">這些版本資訊提供新功能和非安全性更新的相關資訊，這些功能和非安全性更新包含 Microsoft 365 Apps 企業版、Microsoft 365 Apps 商務版，以及 Project 和 Visio 版的傳統型應用程式訂閱版本的半年企業通道更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-104">These release notes provide information about new features and non-security updates that are included in Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel updates for Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise, Microsoft 365 Apps for business, and the subscription versions of the desktop apps for Project and Visio.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-105">我們會變更 Microsoft 365 應用程式的更新通道，包括新增新的更新通道 (每月企業通道)，並變更現有的更新通道名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-105">We’re making some changes to the update channels for Microsoft 365 Apps, including adding a new update channel (Monthly Enterprise Channel) and changing the names of the existing update channels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-106">如需深入了解，[請閱讀本文](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2127441)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-106">To learn more, [read this article](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2127441).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
>
>- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-107">當使用半年企業通道的使用者透過 Office 入口網站下載並安裝 Microsoft 365 Apps 到 Windows 10 上時，OneNote 2016 依預設將包括在其中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-107">OneNote 2016 will now be included by default when a user on the Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel downloads and installs Microsoft 365 Apps on Windows 10 from the Office Portal.</span></span>


[//]: # (DO NOT REMOVE BUGDETAILS CONTENT END)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-113">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-113">Resolved issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-115">我們已修正在圖表中選取資料數列之後，Excel 停止回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-115">We fixed an issue where Excel would stop responding after selecting a data series in a chart.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-116">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-116">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-117">已修正如果文件儲存失敗，可能會導致應用程式非預期關閉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-117">Fixed an issue that could cause the application to close unexpectedly if a document save failed.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-118">解決在某些情況下，選取設計構想會移除簡報的資料分類標籤的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-118">Addresses an issue where selecting a Design Idea removes the presentation's Data Classification Label, in certain cases</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-119">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-119">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-120">已修正如果文件儲存失敗，可能會導致應用程式非預期關閉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-120">Fixed an issue that could cause the application to close unexpectedly if a document save failed.</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-121">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-121">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-122">已修正在商務用 Skype 訊息中複製/貼上時，會導致出現對話方塊顯示「貼上您的內容時發生問題」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-122">Fixed an issue where copy/paste in Skype for Business messages resulted in a dialog displaying "Something went wrong when pasting your content".</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-131">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-131">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-132">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-132">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-133">已修正當開啟具有無效檔案内容 (建立時間、修改時間等) 的 UNC 檔案時，Excel 會意外關閉的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-133">Fixed an issue where Excel would close unexpectedly when opening UNC files that have invalid file attributes (creation time, modified time, etc.)</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-134">我們已修正將圖表從 Excel 複製並貼到 Word 或 PowerPoint 時，小數位和千分位分隔符號設定不會執行的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-134">We fixed an issue where decimal and thousands separators settings would not carry over when copying a chart from Excel and pasting into Word or PowerPoint.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-135">我們已修正執行涉及樞紐分析表範圍格式設定的巨集，在每次執行巨集時效能都會變差的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-135">We fixed an issue where the performance of running a macro involving PivotTable range formatting would get worse each time the macro is run.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-136">我們已修正將工作表複製或移動到另一個活頁簿時，設定格式化的條件規則的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-136">We fixed an issue where conditional formatting rules were dropped when copying or moving sheets to another workbook.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-137">我們已修正當應用程式啟動時停用開始頁面，使用者無法將敏感度標籤套用至 Excel 檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-137">We fixed an issue where users were unable to apply sensitivity labels to Excel files when the start screen on app boot was disabled.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-138">我們已修正從 OneDrive 同步處理資料夾開啟雲端檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-138">We fixed an issue in opening cloud file from OneDrive sync folder.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-139">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-139">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-140">解決在新增或儲存附件時，會導致 Outlook 停止運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-140">Addressed an issue which caused Outlook to stop working sporadically when adding or saving attachments.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-141">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-141">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-142">我們已修正一個問題，即在 QAT 中新增的字型大小命令在更新時，會自動完成到最接近的已定義字型大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-142">We have fixed an issue where font size command, added in QAT, auto completes to the nearest defined font size while updating it.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-143">已修正使用保留來源格式設定選項複製及貼上投影片時，有時會將此設定意外地複製到新的投影片母片的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-143">Fixed an issue where copy and paste of a slide with 'keep source formatting' option would sometimes copy over a new slide master unexpectedly</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-144">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-144">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-145">我們已修正有時開啟 Word 文件可能會顯示錯誤對話方塊的追蹤修訂問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-145">We fixed an issue in Track Changes which sometimes opening Word document might display error dialog.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-146">我們已修正從 OneDrive 同步處理資料夾開啟雲端檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-146">We fixed an issue in opening cloud file from OneDrive sync folder.</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-147">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-147">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-148">已修正無法在 Office 中成功開啟檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-148">Fixed an issue that prevented successful open of a file in Office.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-149">已修正使用複製格式將包含草繪外框的文件套用至連接器可能會損毀的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-149">Fixed an issue where documents containing Sketched outlines applied to connectors via Format Painter could become corrupted.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-166">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-166">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-167">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-167">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-168">**在查詢設計工具、SQL 檢視和關聯視窗中工作時更具生產力：** 在資料表上按一下滑鼠右鍵即可開啟、設計、調整大小及隱藏它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-168">**Be more productive working in Query Designer, SQL view, and the Relationships window:** Right-click a table to open, design, size, and hide it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-169">在 SQL 檢視中搜尋及取代文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-169">Search and replace text in SQL View.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-170">在 [關聯圖] 視窗中選取多個資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-170">Select multiple tables in the Relationships window.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-171">**按幾下就能新增資料表：** 使用 [新增資料表] 工作窗格，當您工作時，該窗格會保持開啟狀態，以便將資料表新增至關聯和查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-171">**Add tables with fewer clicks:** Use the Add Tables task pane, which stays open while you work, to add tables to relationships and queries.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="cf135-172">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-172">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/56eb7df2-8a52-4e90-a7e0-8f891a5c56bd)

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-173">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-173">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-174">**您最愛的 Excel 函數計算速度提升了：** SUMIFS、AVERAGEIFS、COUNTIFS、MAXIFS 和 MINIFS 函數現在比以往更快了。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-174">**Your favorite Excel functions just got faster:** The SUMIFS, AVERAGEIFS, COUNTIFS, MAXIFS, and MINIFS functions are much faster than ever before.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-175">更快速地前往底線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-175">Get to the bottom line more quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-176">立即試用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-176">Try one now.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-177">**RealTimeData (RTD) 的改進** 在 Office 365 版本 2002 的每月通道或更新版本中，Excel RealTimeData (RTD) 函數速度快于 Excel 2010 計算試算表中的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-177">**Realtimedata (RTD) improvements:** In Office 365 version 2002 monthly channel and later, Excel's RealTimeData (RTD) function is much faster than Excel 2010 calculating data in the spreadsheet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-178">我們在其基礎記憶體和資料結構中移除了瓶頸，並使其成為安全執行緒，讓它可在多執行緒重新計算 (MTR) 的所有可用執行緒上計算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-178">We removed bottlenecks in its underlying memory and data structures as well as made it thread-safe to allow  it to be calculated on all available threads of Multithreaded recalculation (MTR).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-179">**改善地圖圖表：** 我們讓地圖圖表變得更好，方法是將地圖圖表與可顯示有關對應位置豐富資訊的 Excel 地理資料類型整合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-179">**Improved map charts:** We've made map charts better by integrating them with Excel's Geographic Data Types, which can reveal rich information about your mapped locations.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="cf135-180">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-180">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/f2cfed55-d622-42cd-8ec9-ec8a358b593b)

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-181">**挑選完美色彩：** 使用十六進位色彩代碼來選擇您想要的字型色彩、文字醒目提示等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-181">**Pick the perfect color:** Use hex color codes to choose exactly the color you want for your font, text highlight, and more.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="cf135-182">在[部落格文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)中查看詳細資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-182">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-183">**在 Excel 中建立來自 Power BI 資料的樞紐分析表：** 您可以在 Excel 中建立樞紐分析表，只要按幾下滑鼠，就能連線到儲存在 Power BI 的樞紐分析表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-183">**Create PivotTables from Datasets in Power BI within Excel:** You can create PivotTables in Excel that are connected to datasets stored in Power BI with a few clicks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-184"> 如此一來，您就能獲得樞紐分析表和 Power BI 的最佳效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-184">Doing this allows you get the best of both PivotTables and Power BI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-185">使用安全 Power BI 資料集的樞紐分析表以計算、摘要及分析資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-185">Calculate, summarize, and analyze your data with PivotTables from your secure Power BI datasets.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="cf135-186">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-186">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/31444a04-9c38-4dd7-9a45-22848c666884)<br /><span data-ttu-id="cf135-187">在[部落格文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)中查看詳細資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-187">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-188">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-188">Outlook</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-250">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-250">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-251">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-251">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-252">已修正使用 [縮放] 視窗時應用程式意外關閉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-252">Fixed an issue where the application would  close unexpectedly when using Zoom window.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-253">此修正會解決嘗試執行之前會產生「查詢太複雜」錯誤訊息的特定查詢的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-253">This fix addresses the issue where trying to run certain queries have previously produced the error message 'Query is too complex'.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-254">此變更可修正當啟動縮放控制方塊 (Shift + F2) 以編輯文字時，可能會導致 Access 意外關閉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-254">This change fixes an issue that could cause Access to to close unexpectedly when launching the Zoom box (Shift + F2) to edit text.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-255">解決插入含有身分識別 (例如，自動編號) 欄位的連結 SQL 資料表的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-255">Resolved an issue with inserting linked SQL tables that include an identity (e.g. autonumber) field.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-256">我們已修正執行查詢的時間大約比預期完成時間兩倍久的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-256">We fixed an issue where query execution was taking approximately twice as long to complete than expected.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-257">已修正問題；您應該可以呼叫日期/時間延伸資料類型至您的程式碼，而不會在您的應用程式中遇到任何問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-257">Fixed an issue to be able to call the Date/Time Extended data type into your code without experiencing any issues in your app.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-258">已修正問題；您現在可以還原為最新的 Access 版本，並使用 DAO/VBA 來管理及編輯十進位資料類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-258">Fixed an issue so you can now revert back to your most updated Access version, and use DAO/VBA to manage and edit a decimal data type.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-259">我們已修正嘗試使用 ODBC DSN 建立器時的錯誤問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-259">We fixed an error issue when trying to use ODBC DSN builder</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-260">已解決此問題 - 您現在可以使用 Office 的隨選即用應用程式外的 ODBC 驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-260">This issue has been resolved - you can now use our ODBC driver outside of Office's Click-to-Run applications.</span></span>


### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-261">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-261">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-262">自動文件分類可能已對處於唯讀模式的活頁簿發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-262">Automatic document classification may have occurred for workbooks that were in read-only mode.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-263">修正若您已從帳戶登出，嘗試建立資料連線時，可能會發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-263">Fixed an issue that could happen when trying to create a data connection if you have signed out from your account.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-264">修正 PivotDateFilter API 中的錯誤，其中的 'Before' 和 'After' 篩選條件是相反的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-264">Fixed a bug with PivotDateFilter APIs in which 'Before' and 'After' filter conditions were reversed.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-265">解決了嘗試將樞紐分析表插入圖表時 Excel 可能會意外關閉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-265">Addressed an issue where Excel may close unexpectedly when attempting to insert PivotTables into a chart sheet.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-266">已修正從 Project 計劃匯出時無法編輯樞紐分析表和無法儲存活頁簿的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-266">Fixed an issue where pivot tables could not be edited and workbooks could not be saved if they were exported from Project plan.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-267">嘗試使用 LET() 函數儲存含有公式的檔案時發生錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-267">An error could occur when trying to save a file that contains a formula using the LET() function.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-268">我們已修正在某些情况下，以唯讀模式開啟文件時會出現多個訊息列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-268">We fixed an issue where in some cases, multiple message bars were appearing when a file was opened in read-only mode.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-269">我們已修正當有許多重複的欄標題值時，大綱子總計可能停止運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-269">We fixed an issue where outline sub-totals could stop working when there were many duplicate column header values.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-270">已修正唯讀書籍在開啟時無法再重新整理樞紐分析表資料的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-270">Fixed an issue where read-only books would no longer refresh pivot table data when opened.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-271">這項變更提供下列問題的修正程式：從 OneDrive 本機同步處理資料夾插入檔案時，Excel 的 [插入物件] 不會顯示正確的圖示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-271">This change provides a fix for the following issue: Excel "Insert Object" does not show correct icon when inserts a file from OneDrive local sync folder.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-272">我們已修正在多執行緒重新計算期間進行群組原則物件更新 (例如，透過遠端群組原則重新整理) 時，Excel 將停止運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-272">We fixed an issue where Excel would stop working when there is a Group Policy Object update (e.g. via Remote Group Policy Refresh) during multithreaded recalc.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-274">當內容從 Excel 複製並使用 [内嵌] 選項貼上到 PowerPoint 中時，改進了 PowerPoint 中的文字字元間距調整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-274">Improved text kerning in PowerPoint when when content is copied from Excel and pasted into PowerPoint with the Embed option.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-294">在 Excel 2016 中使用數位簽章所儲存的活頁簿，會在於目前版本的 Excel 中開啟時導致簽章失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-294">Workbooks saved with a digital signature in Excel 2016 could have the signature invalidated upon opening in the current version of Excel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-305">透過暫時變更建立頁面版本歷程記錄的頻率，可改善同步處理與服務的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-305">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily altering how frequently page version histories are created.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-306">透過暫時將 OneNote 2016 中新嵌入附件的最大允許大小減少為 50MB，來改善同步處理與服務的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-306">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily reducing the maximum allowable size of new embedded attachments to 50MB in OneNote 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-307">對於超過此限制的檔案，使用者可以選擇將檔案上傳到 OneDrive，並將連結插入 OneNote。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-307">For files that exceed this limit, users will have the option of uploading the file to OneDrive and inserting a link into OneNote.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-308">透過暫時停用 OneNote 2016 中的應用程式內視訊錄製，來改善同步處理與服務的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-308">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily disabling in-app video recording in OneNote 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-309">本機筆記本不受這個值的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-309">Local notebooks are not impacted by this measure.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-313">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-313">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-314">我們已修正選用連線體驗導致網頁增益集無法載入的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-314">We fixed an issue where optional connected experiences blocked web add-ins from loading.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cf135-315">請參閱此處的更多詳細資訊： https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/office/blogs/outlook-add-ins-and-optional-connected-experiences/</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-315">See more detail here:  https://developer.microsoft.com/en-us/office/blogs/outlook-add-ins-and-optional-connected-experiences/</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-319">修正導致使用者嘗試從次要帳戶建立會議邀請的問題，讓帳戶新增至他們的個人檔案，而不會看到空白的表格: 是欄位而不是其電子郵件地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-319">Fixes an issue that caused users who attempted to create a meeting request from a secondary account added to their profile to not see a blank From: field instead of their email address.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-321">解決了當代理人在某些情況下遭到拒絕而導致會議無法從經理的行事曆中移除的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-321">Addressed an issue that caused meetings to fail to be removed from a manager's calendar when declined by a delegate in some circumstances.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-322">解決了導致使用 Shared Calendar Improvements 的某些使用者無法查看剛新增的共用行事曆的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-322">Addressed an issue that prevented some users of the Shared Calendar Improvements feature from being able to view a newly-added shared calendar.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-323">解決由於按一下角落中的 [X] 而導致使用者無法關閉共用行事曆的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-323">Addresses an issue that caused users to be unable to close shared calendars by clicking on the "X" in the corner.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-324">解決會導致 [開啟共用行事曆改良] 設定有時候無法套用至現有共用行事曆的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-324">Addresses an issue that caused the "Turn on shared calendar improvements" setting to sometimes fail to apply to existing shared calendars.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-397">已修正 [指派資源] 對話方塊中選取的工作與工作面板檢視中所選工作不同的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-397">Fixed an issue where the task selected in the assign resources dialog isn't the same as the task selected in the task board view.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-461">當您啟用增益集，而登錄金鑰 HKEY_CURRENT_USER \Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth 被設為零時，辦公主機視窗會意外關閉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-461">The office host was  close unexpectedly in windows, when an add-in is being activated while the registry key HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-462">此變更將修正此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-462">This change would fix this issue.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-464">此更新修正了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 中的問題，其中特定 VBA 專案參考了程式庫名稱或程式庫路徑中有 DBCS 字元的程式碼程式庫，因而在載入時被 Office 應用程式視為損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-464">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-465">此更新解決了 Microsoft Office 中的一個問題：可能無法在執行時期正確找到 Visual Basic for Applications 專案，這些專案的參照預期透搜尋 PATH 環境變數指定的位置來找到，進而導致VBA 執行時期錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-465">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Office where Visual Basic for Applications projects with references that are expected to be found by searching locations specified in the PATH environment variable may not be found properly at runtime, leading to VBA runtime errors.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-466">此修正可解決同時防止限制存取和保護設有密碼之檔案的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-466">This fix resolves an error which occurs preventing both restricting access and protecting files with a password simultaneously.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-467">解決會導致從應用程式拖曳部分內容時遇到意外關閉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-467">Resolved an issue that may have caused an unexpected closure when dragging some content from the app.</span></span>



[//]: # (DO NOT REMOVE BUGDETAILS CONTENT END)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-561">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-561">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-562">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-562">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-563">這解決了舊版 Office 中 SQL 資料提供者建立的連結設定內部表格内容與 Office 365 不同的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-563">This addresses an issue where connections created by the SQL data provider in older versions of Office would set internal table properties differently from Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-564">這導致在舊版 Office 中使用 Office 365 開啟文件時，這些檔案的 [表格預覽/查詢編輯器] 下拉清單被停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-564">This caused the Table Preview / Query Editor dropdown to be disabled for files with connections created in older versions of Office when they were opened using Office 365.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-565">已解決筆跡會導致 Excel 無法回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-565">Resolved an issue where inking could cause Excel to become unresponsive.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-566">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-566">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-567">已修正新增共用信箱之後，導致使用者無法連線至公用資料夾的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-567">Fixes an issue that caused users to be unable to connect to Public Folders after adding a shared mailbox.</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-568">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-568">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-569">此變更解決 [壓縮圖片] 對話方塊無法保留特定使用者設定的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-569">This change addresses an issue with the Compress Picture dialog not retaining certain user settings.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-651">**Outlook 中的 [插入連結] 功能表會插入含有租用戶系統管理員所定義的權限的連結：** Outlook 中使用 [插入連結] 所插入的連結，只有具有連結權限的使用者可使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-651">**Insert Link Menu in Outlook will insert a link with permission defined by tenant admin:** A link from the Insert Link MRU in Outlook would insert a link that only worked for users who already had permissions to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-652">這常會造成使用者來回傳送電子郵件，要求對方授與文件的存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-652">This often caused back and forth emails between users asking to be granted access to a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-653">我們已更新這項體驗，現在插入的連結將具有由租用戶系統管理員設定的預設權限。針對 MSIT，這是「組織可以編輯」，使得以此方式收到共用連結的所有內部使用者將可以存取它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-653">We've updated this experience so now the link is inserted with the default permission set by the tenant admin. ### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-745">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-745">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-746">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-746">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-747">此更新會修正使用 ADODB 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-747">This update fixes an issue where using an ADODB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-748">VB 程式碼中的記錄器物件可能會不正確地報告錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-748">Recorder object in VB code may incorrectly report an error.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-749">Access 範本應不再導致資料庫中的附件欄出現故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-749">Access templates should no longer cause attachment columns to fail within a database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-750">個體化範本後，您現在應該可以將附件欄新增至資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-750">After instantiating a template, you should now be able to add an attachment field to your database.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-751">此更新修正可能會導致 Microsoft Access 無法識別連結的 SQL Server 資料表中的識別資料行的問題，這可能會導致不正確地將資料列報告為已刪除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-751">This update fixes an issue that can cause Microsoft Access to fail to identify an Identity Column in a linked SQL Server table, which can cause rows to be reported as deleted incorrectly.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-752">此更新可修正 Microsoft Access 中的「更新查詢」執行時或在 SQL 中使用 UPDATE 陳述式時，可能導致錯誤「查詢已損壞」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-752">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Access that may cause the error "Query is Corrupt" when an Update Query is run, or an UPDATE statement is used in SQL.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-753">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-753">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-754">加速載入本機 OneDrive 資料夾中的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-754">Speed up loading of files that are available on local OneDrive folder.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-755">修正 CUBEVALUE 函數有時會傳回不正確結果的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-755">Fixed an issue where CUBEVALUE functions would sometimes return an incorrect result.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-756">解決開啟內嵌活頁簿時，功能區自訂無法載入的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-756">Resolved an issue with ribbon customization not loading when opening embedded workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-757">在 Word 或 PowerPoint 中重新開啟內嵌的活頁簿時，在某些情況下 Excel 會當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-757">Excel would crash in certain cases when re-opening a workbook embedded in Word or PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-758">修正操作功能表中的註解命令未顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-758">Fixed an issue where comment commands in the context menu were not being displayed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-759">我們已修正樞紐分析圖的右鍵功能表，以啟用 [顯示詳細資料] 選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-759">We fixed the right click menu for Pivot Charts to enable the option to Show Details.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-760">解決在未開啟活頁簿時，搜尋最近使用的檔案會造成當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-760">Resolved an issue that may have caused a crash when searching for recent files while no workbook is open.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-761">修正在相同活頁簿中按一下加入書籤的超連結會導致活頁簿隱藏的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-761">Fixed an issue where clicking a bookmarked hyperlink within the same workbook would cause the workbook to be hidden.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-762">儲存為 CSV 檔案時，在某些情況下，Excel 會將所有欄合併成單一欄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-762">When saving as a CSV file, Excel could merge all columns into a single column in some cases.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-763">在受保護工作表中的範圍使用 Range.ClearContents 可能會比預期花的時間更長。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-763">Using Range.ClearContents on a range in a protected sheet could take longer than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-764">已修正在 [預覽列印] 中顯示表單控制項時的文字縮放比例問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-764">Fixed a problem with scaling of text in form controls when displayed in Print Preview.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-765">與功能區互動的 VBA 宏可能會意外以 ScreenUpdating 設定為 True 執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-765">VBA macros that interact with the ribbon may run with ScreenUpdating set to True unexpectedly.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-766">修正在複製含有樞紐分析表的工作表後，會於某些情況下導致 Excel 當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-766">Fixed an issue which would cause Excel to crash in some cases after copying a sheet containing a PivotTable.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-767">在某些情況下，開啟 CSV 檔案所花費的時間超過預期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-767">Opening CSV files was taking longer than expected in some circumstances.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-768">在某些情況下，當您切換不同縮放比例的活頁簿時，Excel 可能會當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-768">Excel may crash in some circumstances when switching between workbooks with different zoom levels.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-769">已修正 VBA 將值寫入範圍時，速度比預期慢的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-769">Fixed an issue with VBA in which writing values to a range would be slower than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-770">從有色彩篩選的欄複製的資料有時候無法正確貼上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-770">Data copied from a column filtered by color sometimes would not paste properly.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-771">開啟含有許多其他活頁簿 (尤其是含有隱藏視窗) 參照的活頁簿時，速度比預期慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-771">Opening a workbook with references to numerous other workbooks, especially with hidden windows, would be slower than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-772">解決當來源活頁簿關閉時，外部連結在填滿時 (向下填滿、跨表填滿等) 不會更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-772">Addressed an issue where external links don't update on fill (fill down, fill across, etc.) if the source book is& closed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-773">修正透過 Teams 共用 Excel 視窗時，使用 Ctrl+Shift+方向鍵來捲動之後，可能會使得 Excel 未回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-773">Fixed an issue where Excel could become unresponsive after using Ctrl+Shift+Arrow keys to scroll when the Excel window is shared through Teams.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-774">在 Excel 2016 中使用數位簽章所儲存的活頁簿，會在於目前版本的 Excel 中開啟時導致簽章失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-774">Workbooks saved with a digital signature in Excel 2016 could have the signature invalidated upon opening in the current version of Excel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-775">解決在儲存並重新開啟檔案時，圖表軸上的「值置於」屬性非預期變更的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-775">Addresses an issue where the "Value Crosses At" property on chart axis unexpectedly changes when saving and re-opening a file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-776">修正儲存至 SharePoint/OneDrive 時，會導致將自訂功能區索引標籤的 CustomUI XML 移除的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-776">Fixed an issue which caused CustomUI XML for a custom ribbon tab to be removed when saving to SharePoint/OneDrive.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-777">改善刪除具有合併儲存格的欄時的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-777">Improved performance when deleting columns with merged cells.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-778">修正 [列印] 對話方塊的印表機清單中，印表機名稱可能會重複的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-778">Fixed an issue where printer names could be repeated in the list of printers in the Print dialog.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-779">修正當檔案路徑太長時，在重新開啟檔案後，外部連結會停止運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-779">Fixed an issue where the external link stops working after the file is reopened if the file path is too long.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-780">已修正列印時表單控制項的核取方塊縮放的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-780">Fixed a problem with the scaling of checkboxes in form controls when printed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-781">當您使用舊版的「共用活頁簿」模式，嘗試為活頁簿的新工作表列出變更時，就會發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-781">A crash could occur when trying to list changes on a new sheet for a workbook using legacy "Shared Workbook" mode.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-782">在已篩選清單中插入欄的時間會比預期更長。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-782">Inserting a column in a filtered list would take longer than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-783">我們已修正某些複製和貼上的圖表連結使用的是對應磁碟機位址，而不是通用位址的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-783">We fixed an issue where some copy and pasted chart links used mapped drive addresses rather than universal addresses.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-784">修正因為增益集是以字母順序載入，而不是以使用者指定的順序載入，而顯示 [這個活頁簿目前正由其他活頁簿所參考中，不可關閉] 錯誤訊息的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-784">Fixed an issue where the error message “This workbook is currently referenced by another and cannot be closed” would appear because add-ins were being loaded in alphabetical order rather than in a user specified order.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-785">修正按一下已開啟活頁簿中某個位置的超連結時，活頁簿可能會隱藏的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-785">Fixed an issue where a workbook could become hidden when clicking a hyperlink to a spot within an already opened workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-786">開啟含有許多其他活頁簿 (尤其是含有隱藏視窗) 參照的活頁簿時，速度比預期慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-786">Opening a workbook with references to numerous other workbooks, especially with hidden windows, would be slower than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-787">使用 VBA 應用程式的 Application.Evaluate 在某些情況下，對使用者定義的函數無法運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-787">Using VBA's Application.Evaluate was not working for User-defined functions in some cases.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-788">修正某些使用者使用內嵌和連結物件 (OLE) 時可能發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-788">Fixed an issue that some users may have experienced with embedded and linked objects (OLE).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-789">使用者在使用某些非英文字元集的情況下，儲存變更時可能會遇到錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-789">Users may encounter an error when saving changes while using some non-English character sets.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-790">此更新可修正會導致資料編輯列以較預期不同的字型顯示文字的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-790">This update fixes an issue that caused the formula bar to display text in a different font than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-791">使用者在使用某些非英文字元集的情況下，儲存變更時可能會遇到錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-791">Users may encounter an error when saving changes while using some non-English character sets.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-792">解決捲動後選取儲存格時，可能導致選取錯誤儲存格的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-792">Resolved an issue where selecting a cell after scrolling could result in the wrong cell being selected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-793">使用者在存取隱藏的命名範圍時可能會遇到錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-793">Users may encounter an error when accessing a hidden named range.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-794">從不受信任的網路共用編輯受保護的檔案時，Excel 可能會發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-794">Excel may have issues when editing a protected file from an untrusted network share.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-795">某些當地語系化版本的 [文字到欄] 功能可能會失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-795">Text to Column functionality may fail for some localizations.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-796">解決從範本建立圖表時的效能問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-796">Addresses a performance issue when creating charts from templates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-797">修正對具有溢出陣列之儲存格進行資料剖析的轉換時，導致某些使用者發生當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-797">Fixed an issue that caused some users to experience crashes when converting text to columns with cells that have a spilling array.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-798">使用 Range.Value 和 Range.Value2 (VBA) 會導致公式以動態陣列的形式輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-798">Using a Range.Value and Range.Value2 (VBA) would cause formulas to be entered as dynamic arrays.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-799">修正公式開頭的 @ 符號會被視為隱含交集運算子的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-799">Fixed an issue where an @ symbol starting a formula would be considered an implicit intersection operator.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-800">我們已修正包含多個含有定義名稱的公式，會導致儲存檔案時間加長的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-800">We fixed an issue where worksheets containing multiple formulas with defined names was resulting in longer times when saving files.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-801">此變更利用軟體轉譯，以避免特定 Intel 圖形驅動程式的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-801">This change circumvents a problem with certain Intel graphics drivers by leveraging software rendering.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-802">解決重新命名簽名時，會導致使用者遇到當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-802">Addresses an issue that caused users to experience crashes when renaming a signature.</span></span>

### <a name="onenote"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-803">OneNote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-803">OneNote</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-804">透過暫時調整 OneNote 2016 中的同步處理頻率，來改善同步處理與服務的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-804">Improve sync and service stability by temporarily adjusting sync frequency in OneNote 2016.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-805">透過暫時延遲下載線上筆記本中內嵌的檔案和影像，直到使用者瀏覽至 OneNote 2016 中的頁面，來改善同步處理與服務的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-805">Improve sync and service stability by temporarily deferring the downloading of embedded files and images in online notebooks until the user navigates to the page in OneNote 2016.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-806">透過暫時停用 OneNote 2016 中的資源回收筒，來改善同步處理與服務的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-806">Improve sync and service stability by temporarily disabling the recycle bin in OneNote 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-807">當使用者嘗試刪除通常會傳送到 [資源回收筒] 的資料時，系統會詢問使用者是否希望保留或永久刪除資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-807">When a user tries to delete data that would normally be sent to the recycle bin, users will be asked if they would prefer to keep or permanently delete the data.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-808">透過暫時將 OneNote 2016 中版本歷程記錄頁面的數目和同步處理頻率降低，來改善同步處理與服務的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-808">Improve sync and service stability by temporarily reducing the number and sync frequency of version history pages in OneNote 2016.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-809">顯示通知，讓使用者可以了解更多 OneNote 使用者體驗中正在採取的臨時措施的資訊，以改善同步處理和服務穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-809">Display a notification that allows the user to learn more about temporary measures being enacted in the OneNote user experience to improve sync and service stability.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-810">透過暫時將 OneNote 2016 中新嵌入附件的最大允許大小減少為 50 MB，來改善同步處理與服務的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-810">Improve sync and service stability by temporarily reducing the maximum allowable size of new embedded attachments to 50MB in OneNote 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-811">對於超過此限制的檔案，使用者可以選擇將檔案上傳到 OneDrive，並將連結插入 OneNote。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-811">For files that exceed this limit, users will have the option of uploading the file to OneDrive and inserting a link into OneNote.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-812">透過暫時停用 OneNote 2016 中的應用程式內視訊錄製，來改善同步處理與服務的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-812">Improve sync and service stability by temporarily disabling in-app video recording in OneNote 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-813">本機筆記本不受這個測量的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-813">Local notebooks are not impacted by this measure.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-814">對通知進行本地化，讓使用者可以了解更多 OneNote 使用者體驗中正在採取的臨時措施的資訊，以改善同步處理和服務穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-814">Localises the notification that allows the user to learn more about temporary measures being enacted in the OneNote user experience to improve sync and service stability.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-816">我們已修正以下問題：當使用多個不同解析度的監視器時，輸入法編輯器 (IEM) 視窗會覆蓋透過 IME 輸入的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-816">We fixed an issue where the IME (Input Method Editor) window would overlap the underlying text being entered via the IME when using multiple monitors with different resolutions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-819">解決會導致網頁增益集存取數位版權管理訊息的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-819">Addresses an issue that caused web add ins to access Digital Rights Managed messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-820">解決會導致週期性約會或會議在接近時區定義變更時於錯誤的時間顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-820">Addresses an issue that caused recurring appointments or meetings to be displayed at the wrong time when approaching a timezone definition change.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-821">在 2019 年使用巴西時區時，週期性會議和約會以 2020 年的錯誤時段顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-821">When using the Brazilia time zone in the year 2019, recurring meetings and appointments are displayed in the wrong timeslot for the year 2020.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-822">此變更與設定使用巴西時區的用戶端或設定使用該時區的會議和約會相關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-822">This change is relevant for clients set in the Brazilia time zone or for meetings and appointments set in that time zone.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="cf135-823">此變更會允許 Outlook 覆寫 Outlook 所使用的特定時區設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-823">This change allows Outlook to override certain time zone settings used by Outlook.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-824">若要叫用時區覆寫，您必須為目前的使用者設定登錄機碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-824">In order to invoke a time zone override you must set a registry key for the current user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-825">登錄機碼名稱必須符合時區的內部名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-825">The registry key name must match the internal name of the time zone.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-826">值表示時區規則的年，用來取代生效年。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-826">The value indicates the time zone rule's year to be used in place of the effective year.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-827">例如，下列登錄機碼覆寫值將使用巴西時區規則做為 2020 年的生效規則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-827">For example, the following registry key override value will use the Brazilia time zone rule for the year 2020 as the effective rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-828">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\TimeZoneOverride]"E.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-828">HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\TimeZoneOverride]"E.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-829">South America Standard Time"=dword:000007e4.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-829">South America Standard Time"=dword:000007e4.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-856">解決會導致協力廠商應用程式無法傳送電子郵件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-856">Addresses an issue that caused third party applications to be unable to send email.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-928">此更新可修正在檢視或撰寫郵件時，Microsoft Outlook 未顯示目前的敏感度標籤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-928">This update fixes an issue with Microsoft Outlook not displaying the current sensitivity label when viewing or composing messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-929">修正在 Word/Excel/PowerPoint 中開啟來自相同 SharePoint 文件庫的多個文件時，僅掃描開啟的第一個文件是否符合原則的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-929">Fixes an issue when multiple documents are open in Word/Excel/PowerPoint from the same SharePoint library, only the first document opened will be scanned for Policy compliance.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-930">為了保護 Office 客戶的安全性，我們現在專門使用 SHA-2 演算法來簽署 Microsoft Office 更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-930">To protect Office customers’ security, Microsoft Office updates are now signed using the SHA-2 algorithm exclusively.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-931">當您啟用增益集，而登錄金鑰 HKEY_CURRENT_USER \Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth 被設為零時，辦公主機視窗會關閉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-931">The office host was closing in windows, when an add-in is being activated while the registry key  HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-932">此變更將修正此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-932">This change would fix this issue.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-933">解決 Access 和 Publisher 因所安裝的語言而無法正常啟動的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-933">Resolved the issue where Access and Publisher might not boot correctly depending on which languages were installed.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-940">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-940">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-941">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-941">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-942">此更新修正彙總 (例如 Sum) 可能會將結果截斷成整數值的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-942">This update fixes an issue where aggregate like Sum may truncate the result to an integer value.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-943">此更新修正包含參照遠端桌面 (例如 SQL Server 桌面) 的聯集查詢可能造成 Access 關閉並重新啟動的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-943">This update fixes an issue where a Union query that includes references to remote tables (e.g. SQL Server tables) may cause Access to close and restart.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-944">此更新可修正 Microsoft Access 中的「更新查詢」執行時或在 SQL 中使用 UPDATE 陳述式時，可能導致錯誤「查詢已損壞」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-944">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Access that may cause the error "Query is Corrupt" when an Update Query is run, or an UPDATE statement is used in SQL.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-945">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-945">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-946">文件標題的荷蘭文按鍵提示已變更為 Alt-G。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-946">Dutch keytip for document title has been changed to Alt-G.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-947">修正在 Excel 中指派給圖形或表單控制項的巨集可能顯示不正確的錯誤訊息，或者可能會處理不正確目標範圍的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-947">Fixed an issue in Excel where macros assigned to shapes or form controls may show incorrect error message, or may work on incorrect target ranges.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-948">解決「尋找及取代」在找到第一個項目後，對話方塊中的焦點位置變更的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-948">Resolved an issue with Find and Replace that change where the focus was in the dialog after finding the first item.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-949">此更新修正在與其他使用者共同撰寫的工作階段中變更樞紐分析表排序的方式，然後重新整理可能觸發當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-949">This fixes an issue where changing the way a PivotTable is sorted and refreshing it while in a coauthoring session with other users could trigger a crash.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-950">我們已修正當 OLAP 樞紐分析表的篩選條件設定為已從 cube 移除的值時會發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-950">We fixed a problem when the filter for an OLAP PivotTable was set to a value that had been removed from the cube.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-951">此更新已修正使用 VBA 將影像新增到圖表的頁首/頁尾時發生錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-951">This update fixes an issue that caused an error to occur whenever VBA was used to add an image to the header/footer of a chart.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-952">我們已修正當變更系列集合時，可能會導致散佈折線圖無法正確呈現的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-952">We fixed an issue which could have caused scatter line charts from rendering properly when changing the series collection</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-953">修正以校正使用圖表範本插入圖表時，預覽中使用的色彩。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-953">Fix to correct colors used in previews when inserting charts using chart templates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-954">已解決當插入或刪除儲存格時，瀑布圖和漏斗圖無法與表格同步處理的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-954">Resolved an issue that caused Waterfall and Funnel charts to get out of sync with tables when cells were inserted or deleted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-955">修正 Excel 中合併衝突的問題，此問題會造成提示使用者重新開啟活頁簿以取得變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-955">Fixed a merge conflict issue in Excel that would result in users being prompted to reopen workbook to pick up the changes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-956">已解決造成執行階段錯誤啟動最小化視窗的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-956">Resolved an issue that caused a macro run-time error activating minimized windows.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-957">解決了開啟內嵌活頁簿時，功能區自訂無法載入的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-957">Resolved an issue with ribbon customization not loading when opening embedded workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-958">已解決導致表格旁的剪下並貼上作業在與其他人共同撰寫時失敗的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-958">Resolved an issue that caused cut and paste operations next to a table to fail when co-authoring with others.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-959">解決使用執行中巨集變更自訂屬性時，會導致共同撰寫中斷的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-959">Resolved an issue that caused co-authoring interruptions when changing custom properties with running macros.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-960">發生您無法從增益集開啟的 WPF (Windows Presentation Foundation) 表單的下拉式方塊選取項目的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-960">There was a problem in which you would be unable to select items from combo box of a WPF (Windows Presentation Foundation) form that was opened by an add-in.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-961">解決在未開啟活頁簿時，搜尋最近使用的檔案會造成當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-961">Resolved an issue that may have caused a crash when searching for recent files while no workbook is open.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-962">修正在預覽列印或列印時，群組方塊控制項的框線無法顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-962">Fixed an issue where the border of a Group Box control wasn't visible in print preview or when printed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-963">修正當活頁簿中有外部連結時，有些使用者可能會遇到多個快顯視窗的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-963">Fixed an issue where some users may have experienced multiple pop-up windows when external links were present in the workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-964">已修正使用者在使用 VBA 巨集清除範圍內容時可能遇到的效能問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-964">Fixed a performance issue that users may have experienced when using a VBA macro to clear the contents of a range.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-965">已修正 VBA 將值寫入範圍時，速度比預期慢的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-965">Fixed an issue with VBA in which writing values to a range would be slower than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-966">解決在儲存並重新開啟檔案時，圖表軸上的「值置於」屬性非預期變更的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-966">Addresses an issue where the "Value Crosses At" property on chart axis unexpectedly changes when saving and re-opening a file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-967">在 Excel 2016 中使用數位簽章所儲存的活頁簿，會在於目前版本的 Excel 中開啟時導致簽章失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-967">Workbooks saved with a digital signature in Excel 2016 could have the signature invalidated upon opening in the current version of Excel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-968">已修正在刪除包含合併儲存格的資料行時，會導致效能變慢的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-968">Fixed an issue which led to slow performance when deleting columns that contain merged cells.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-969">已修正在 [預覽列印] 中顯示表單控制項時的文字縮放比例問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-969">Fixed a problem with scaling of text in form controls when displayed in Print Preview.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-970">將依色彩篩選的資料複製到具有不同寬度的欄時，值無法貼上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-970">When copying data filtered by color to a column with a different width, the values would not be pasted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-971">已修正當 Excel 視窗透過 Teams 共用時，使用 Ctrl + Shift + 方向鍵滑動後，Excel 可能會無法回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-971">Fixed an issue where Excel could become unresponsive after using Ctrl+Shift+Arrow keys to scroll when the Excel window is shared through Teams.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-972">已修正列印時表單控制項的核取方塊縮放的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-972">Fixed a problem with the scaling of checkboxes in form controls when printed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-973">修正在相同活頁簿中按一下加入書籤的超連結會導致活頁簿隱藏的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-973">Fixed an issue where clicking a bookmarked hyperlink within the same workbook would cause the workbook to be hidden.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-974">當您使用舊版的「共用活頁簿」模式，嘗試為活頁簿的新工作表列出變更時，就會發生當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-974">A crash could occur when trying to list changes on a new sheet for a workbook using legacy "Shared Workbook" mode.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-975">[資料剖析] 功能對某些地區設定可能會失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-975">Text to Column functionality may fail for some locales.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-976">使用者在存取隱藏的命名範圍時可能會遇到錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-976">Users may encounter an error when accessing a hidden named range.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-977">使用者在使用某些非英文字元集的情況下，儲存變更時可能會遇到錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-977">Users may encounter an error when saving changes while using some non-English character sets.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-978">已修正圖表標題中影像檔案大小在儲存包含圖表的活頁簿時增加的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-978">Fixed an issue where the file size of images in chart headers increased when the workbook containing the chart was saved.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-979">非同步使用者定義函數造成的效能問題，導致它們同步執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-979">Performance issue with Asynchronous User-Defined Functions that was causing them to be run Synchronously.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-980">已大幅改善刪除有合併儲存格之欄的效能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-980">Significant improvements to the performance of deleting columns with merged cells.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-981">解決捲動後選取儲存格時，可能導致選取錯誤儲存格的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-981">Resolved an issue where selecting a cell after scrolling could result in the wrong cell being selected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-982">已解決 Lookup 函數可能會傳回錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-982">Resolved an issue where the Lookup function may return an error.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-983">已修正以下問題：將選取範圍與交互參照的活頁簿保持同步時，導致交互參照的活頁簿中的 DBCS 字元損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-983">Fixed an issue that causes corruption of DBCS characters in cross referenced books by keeping the selection ranges in sync with the cross referenced book.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-985">當檔案具備大量設定格式化的條件時，按一下 [字型色彩] 按鈕時出現的效能緩慢問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-985">Issue with slow performance on clicking on the Font Color button when a file has extensive conditional formatting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-987">從不受信任的網路共用編輯受保護的檔案時，Excel 可能會發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-987">Excel may have issues when editing a protected file from an untrusted network share.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-989">解決在目前的 Office 版本中開啟在舊版 Office 中建立的活頁簿時，可能導致 Excel 懸置的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-989">Resolved an issue where workbooks created in earlier versions of Office could cause Excel to hang when opened in current versions of Office.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-992">這項變更透過利用軟體轉譯避免特定 Intel 圖形驅動程式發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-992">This change circumvents a problem with certain Intel graphics drivers by leveraging software rendering.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-995">已修正在 Excel 構想功能中，在 Win32 用戶端中按一下 [構想] 按鈕來載入增益集時會發生錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-995">Fix issue in Excel Ideas feature, error when loading the add-in by clicking the Ideas button in Win32 client.</span></span> 

### <a name="onenote"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-996">OneNote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-996">OneNote</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-997">對通知進行本地化，讓使用者可以了解更多 OneNote 使用者體驗中正在採取的臨時措施的資訊，以改善同步處理和服務穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-997">Localizes the notification that allows the user to learn more about temporary measures being enacted in the OneNote user experience to improve sync and service stability.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-998">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-998">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-999">來自 Outlook 郵件中的 cid: 影像連結現在能在要求時成功中斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-999">The links of cid: images from Outlook messages can now be successfully broken when requested.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1000">修正使用者將信箱從基本驗證升級為新式驗證後，造成將錯誤的帳戶與其 Outlook 設定檔相關聯的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1000">Fixed an issue where users having their mailbox upgraded from basic to modern authentication were ending up with the wrong account associated with their Outlook profile.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1001">解決會導致網頁增益集在不該存取數位版權管理訊息時進行存取的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1001">Addresses an issue that caused web add ins to access Digital Rights Managed messages when they should not.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1076">我們已修正表格中「最適文字大小」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1076">We fixed an issue in Fit Text in Table.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1077">我們已修正追蹤修訂有時候會進入無限迴圈的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1077">We fixed an issue in track changes that sometimes go into infinite loop.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1078">我們已修正在某些情況下，儲存現有檔案永遠會導致出現 [另存新檔] 對話方塊且檔案永遠不會儲存的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1078">We fixed an issue where in some cases, saving an existing file always causes the Save As dialog and the file never actually saves.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1079">我們已修正將兩份文件合併成一份文件時的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1079">We fixed an issue when merging 2 documents into one document.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1080">修正受保護無法編輯之文件的比較功能問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1080">Fixed an issue with Compare feature for documents that were protected for editing.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1081">修正應用程式可能在關機時懸置的各種問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1081">Fixes various issues where the app may hang on shutdown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1082">同時修正特定相關增益集當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1082">Also fixes certain add-in related crashes.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1083">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1083">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1084">已修正不正確地將平假名和漢字中的日本新年號 "Reiwa" (令和) 識別為拼字錯誤或不合文法的運算式的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1084">Fixed an issue of incorrectly identifying the new era name “Reiwa” in Hiragana and Kanji as a misspelled or ungrammatical expression.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1085">已修正嘗試共用儲存在 SharePoint 2016 上的檔案時，導致使用者遇到「很抱歉，發生問題，無法共用」訊息的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1085">Fixed an issue which caused users to get this message "Sorry, something is preventing us from sharing this" when trying to share files stored on SharePoint 2016.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1086">已修正在 PowerPoint 共同撰寫和離線編輯的工作階段中可能會導致資料遺失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1086">Fixed issue that could cause data loss in sessions that involved both coauthoring and offline editing in PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1087">修正使用者在開啟檔案時可能會遇到的當機問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1087">This is a fix for a crash that users could hit on opening a file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1088">在某些情況下，同步處理引擎備份的 SharePoint 檔案可能會顯示「已儲存」但實際上未儲存任何變更，導致資料遺失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1088">In some instances, a sync-engine backed sharepoint file could show 'Saved' but not have actually saved any changes, resulting in data loss.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1089">解決使用者可能無法儲存 Word、Excel 和 PowerPoint 文件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1089">Resolved an issue where users may be unable to save Word, Excel, and PowerPoint documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1090">此問題會影響建立新檔案並在按一下 [儲存] 圖示或按 Ctrl + S 之後帶出 [另存成模型對話方塊] 選項的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1090">This issue affects users that create a new file and bring up the "Save as Dialog" option after clicking on the Save icon or pressing Ctrl + S.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1091">從已過時的 API 中移除 Word，以修正其當機問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1091">Fixes a crash in Word by moving away from a deprecated API.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1092">修正 PowerPoint 中半形片假名字元在垂直文字方塊中無法正確旋轉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1092">Fixing an issue where half-width katakana characters were not rotating properly when in vertical text boxes in PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1093">已修正 Win7 的效能問題，其中，於所有應用程式中從功能區插入圖案庫時，大約需要 4 秒鐘的時間才會顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1093">Fixed a perf issue on Win7 where the insert shapes gallery from the ribbon in all apps took approximately 4 seconds to appear.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1094">已修正 Backstage 的 [資訊位置] 平板未顯示協助工具資訊的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1094">Fixed a bug where accessibility information was not being displayed in the Info Place slab of the backstage.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1095">改善有關登錄完整性的 Office 更新程序的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1095">Improves reliability of the Office update process concerning registry integrity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1096">我們已將 2019 年 1 月和 7 月分支的通道名稱更新為新通道名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1096">We have updated the channel names for the January and July 2019 forks to the new channel names.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1097">更正可能會在計量網路上非預期封鎖更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1097">Corrects an issue where updates may have been unexpectedly blocked on metered networks.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1098">修正相對期限只有在第一次設定時才會有效的 ODT 和 GPO 更新期限設定中的錯誤 (bug)。此修正可啟用後續更新的相關期限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1098">Fix to bug in ODT and GPO Update Deadline setting where relative deadline only works the first time it is set, the fix enables the relative deadline for subsequent updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1099">某些情況下，Office 快速鍵可能會在更新後消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1099">In certain circumstances, Office shortcuts may disappear following an update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1100">此更新可改善發佈 Office 快速鍵時的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1100">This update improves reliability when publishing of Office shortcuts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1101">解決 Office 更新可能會非預期地從 Office CDN 而不是預期使用的來源 (例如本機或網路共用或 Configuration Manager 提供的位置) 下載檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1101">Resolves an issue where Office updates may have unexpectedly downloaded files from the Office CDN instead of the intended source, such as a local or network share, or Configuration Manager-provided location.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1102">解決在某些情況下，若使用者不是系統管理員且系統帳戶沒有網路連線時，將無法套用更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1102">Resolves an issue where an update would not apply in certain cases where the user is not an administrator and the System account did not have network connectivity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1103">已修正 Office 更新訊息不以預期語言顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1103">Fixed an issue where Office update messages appear in a different language than expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1104">自此以後，Office 更新訊息會正確符合 Windows 顯示語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1104">Going forward, Office update messages will correctly match the Windows display language.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1105">下載 Office 更新時透過繼續之前可能已中斷的下載，藉此改善可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1105">Improved reliability when downloading Office updates by resuming downloads which may have been previously interrupted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1106">解決第三方外掛程式中與文字方塊/圖案自動調整屬性相關的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1106">Address issues related to Textbox/Shape Autofit property in third-party plug-ins.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1107">此變更可解決開啟損毀的檔案之後，正確呈現影像的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1107">This change addresses correctly rendering images after opening a corrupted file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1108">此變更可解決轉譯某些含有標記的散佈圖緩慢的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1108">This change addresses slow rendering of some scatter charts with markers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1109">我們已修正大型樹狀檢視可能會導致當機的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1109">We fixed an issue where large tree views could result in a crash</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1110">此更新修正了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 中的問題，其中特定 VBA 專案參考了程式庫名稱或程式庫路徑中有 DBCS 字元的程式碼程式庫，因而在載入時被 Office 應用程式視為損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1110">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1111">為了保護 Office 客戶的安全性，我們現在專門使用 SHA-2 演算法來簽署 Microsoft Office 更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1111">To protect Office customers' security, Microsoft Office updates are now signed using the SHA-2 algorithm exclusively.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1112">為了保護 Office 客戶的安全性，我們現在專門使用 SHA-2 演算法來簽署 Microsoft Office 更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1112">To protect Office customers' security, Microsoft Office updates are now signed using the SHA-2 algorithm exclusively.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1242">已修正在預覽列印或列印時群組方塊控制項的框線無法顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1242">Fixed an issue where the border of a Group Box control wasn't visible in print preview or when printed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1245">已修正以下問題：將選取範圍與交互參照的活頁簿保持同步時，導致交互參照的活頁簿中的 DBCS 字元損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1245">Fixed an issue that causes corruption of DBCS characters in cross referenced books by keeping the selection ranges in sync with the cross referenced book.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1246">已解決使用自動調整來調整列高時，核取方塊可能收縮的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1246">Resolved an issue that could cause check box controls to shrink when using autofit to adjust row height.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1247">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1247">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1250">已解決導致使用者在啟動 Outlook 時，「正在載入設定檔」畫面時停滯的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1250">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a hang at the Loading Profile screen when Outlook is starting up.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1251">已解決導致使用者在變更檢視時發生當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1251">Addressed an issue that caused users to see intermittent crashes when changing views.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1252">已解決在 Citrix 環境中檢視 30 個以上的行事曆時，導致使用者遇到當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1252">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a crash when viewing more than 30 calendars in a Citrix environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1253">[此處](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3141476/outlook-may-crash-when-you-view-more-than-30-calendars-in-a-calen)是記錄舊版問題的個別 KB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1253">[Here](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3141476/outlook-may-crash-when-you-view-more-than-30-calendars-in-a-calen) is the individual KB where this was documented for previous versions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1254">已解決以下問題：使用者將共用行事曆資料夾同步到 OST 時發生問題，這導致嘗試與這些資料夾互動時發生權限錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1254">Addresses an issue that caused users to have problems problems with shared calendar folders syncing to the OST, resulting in permission errors when they try to interact with these folders.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1255">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1255">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1256">已改善複製貼上的案例，即將 PowerPoint 投影片中的圖形複製並貼到其他投影片可能會因為異常而失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1256">Improved a copy-paste scenario Copying the Shape in powerpoint slide and paste it in other slide in a loop might fail with exception.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1257">已修正導致共同作業使用者之間效能較低的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1257">Fixed an issue that was causing slower performance between collaboration users.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1258">已修正以下問題：當檔案以漸進式開啟時，若其中一個投影片包含多個內嵌媒體串流可能會發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1258">Fixed an issue that can occur when a file being opened incrementally contains a slide with more than one embedded media stream.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1259">已修正以下問題：首次啟動 PowerPoint 時，不受信任的增益集可能不會顯示安全性警告訊息列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1259">We fixed an issue where security warning message bar may not appear for untrusted add-ins on first launch of PowerPoint.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1260">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1260">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1261">已修正以下問題：由於基準行事曆變更時未更新資源行事曆，而導致時程表和專案計劃之間的實際工作可能不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1261">Fixed an issue where actual work may be different between the timesheet and project plan due to resource calendars not being updated when the base calendar changes.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1334">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1334">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1335">**較佳變形效果：** 命名您的圖形以便加強掌控其轉化方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1335">**Better shapeshifting:** Name your shapes for more control over how they morph.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="cf135-1336">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1336">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/bc7f48ff-f152-4ee8-9081-d3121788024f)
