### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1413">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1413">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1414">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1414">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1415">此更新修正彙總 (例如 Sum) 可能會將結果截斷成整數值的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1415">This update fixes an issue where aggregate like Sum may truncate the result to an integer value.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1416">此更新修正包含參照遠端桌面 (例如 SQL Server 桌面) 的聯集查詢可能造成 Access 關閉並重新啟動的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1416">This update fixes an issue where a Union query that includes references to remote tables (e.g. SQL Server tables) may cause Access to close and restart.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1417">此更新可修正 Microsoft Access 中的「更新查詢」執行時或在 SQL 中使用 UPDATE 陳述式時，可能導致發生錯誤「查詢已損壞」&quot;&quot;的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1417">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Access that may cause the error &quot;Query is Corrupt&quot; when an Update Query is run, or an UPDATE statement is used in SQL.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1418">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1418">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1419">文件標題的荷蘭文按鍵提示已變更為 Alt-G。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1419">Dutch keytip for document title has been changed to Alt-G.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1420">修正在 Excel 中指派給圖形或表單控制項的巨集可能顯示不正確的錯誤訊息，或者可能會處理不正確目標範圍的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1420">Fixed an issue in Excel where macros assigned to shapes or form controls may show incorrect error message, or may work on incorrect target ranges.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1421">解決「尋找及取代」在找到第一個項目後，對話方塊中的焦點位置變更的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1421">Resolved an issue with Find and Replace that change where the focus was in the dialog after finding the first item.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1422">此更新修正在與其他使用者共同撰寫的工作階段中變更樞紐分析表排序的方式，然後重新整理可能觸發當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1422">This fixes an issue where changing the way a PivotTable is sorted and refreshing it while in a coauthoring session with other users could trigger a crash.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1423">我們已修正當 OLAP 樞紐分析表的篩選條件設定為已從 cube 移除的值時會發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1423">We fixed a problem when the filter for an OLAP PivotTable was set to a value that had been removed from the cube.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1424">修正以校正使用圖表範本插入圖表時，預覽中使用的色彩。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1424">Fix to correct colors used in previews when inserting charts using chart templates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1425">我們已修正當變更系列集合時，可能會導致散佈折線圖無法正確呈現的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1425">We fixed an issue which could have caused scatter line charts from rendering properly when changing the series collection.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1426">已解決當插入或刪除儲存格時，瀑布圖和漏斗圖無法與表格同步處理的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1426">Resolved an issue that caused Waterfall and Funnel charts to get out of sync with tables when cells were inserted or deleted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1427">修正 Excel 中合併衝突的問題，此問題會造成提示使用者重新開啟活頁簿以取得變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1427">Fixed a merge conflict issue in Excel that would result in users being prompted to reopen workbook to pick up the changes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1428">解決了開啟內嵌活頁簿時，功能區自訂無法載入的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1428">Resolved an issue with ribbon customization not loading when opening embedded workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1431">已解決導致表格旁的剪下並貼上作業在與其他人共同撰寫時失敗的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1431">Resolved an issue that caused cut and paste operations next to a table to fail when co-authoring with others.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1433">發生您無法從增益集開啟的 WPF (Windows Presentation Foundation) 表單的下拉式方塊選取項目的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1433">There was a problem in which you would be unable to select items from combo box of a WPF (Windows Presentation Foundation) form that was opened by an add-in.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1439">解決在目前的 Office 版本中開啟在舊版 Office 中建立的活頁簿時，可能導致 Excel 懸置的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1439">Resolved an issue where workbooks created in earlier versions of Office could cause Excel to hang when opened in current versions of Office.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1445">當在增益集管理員中瀏覽時，顯示 16 個以上的增益集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1445">Enabled more than 16 add-ins to show when browsing in the add-in manager.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1446">這項變更透過利用軟體轉譯避免特定 Intel 圖形驅動程式發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1446">This change circumvents a problem with certain Intel graphics drivers by leveraging software rendering.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1447">來自 Outlook 郵件中的 cid: 影像連結現在能在要求時成功中斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1447">The links of cid: images from Outlook messages can now be successfully broken when requested.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1488">此變更還原 PowerPoint 影片控制項的協助工具名稱的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1488">This change restores the accessible name for PowerPoint video controls.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1489">我們已修正部分動畫無法開始的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1489">We fixed an issue which could prevent some animations from starting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1490">我們已修正將投影片從一個簡報複製到另一個簡報時可能會造成母片重複的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1490">We fixed an issue when copying a slide from one presentation to another might create duplicate masters.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1491">如果在不支援的版本中開啟含有新的新式註解的檔案，將會顯示黃色警告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1491">Files with new modern comments will show a yellow warning if opened in unsupported version</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1492">可靠性修正：已修正第三方增益集可能會造成 PowerPoint 當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1492">Reliability fix: Fixed an issue where third party add-in might crash PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1493">已修正 PowerPoint 中半形片假名字元在垂直文字方塊中無法正確旋轉的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1493">Fixed an issue where half-width katakana characters were not rotating properly when in vertical text boxes in PowerPoint.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1494">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1494">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1495">修正讓 Windows 7 上的使用者能夠從 Project Web App 和 SharePoint 網站開啟專案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1495">Fixed an issue to enable users on Windows 7 to be able to open projects from Project Web App and SharePoint sites.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1496">發現在開啟唯讀專案時，使用者可能會收到數個訊息的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1496">Identified an issue where users could get several messages when opening a read-only project.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1497">「全部撫平」命令無法正確解決資源過度分派的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1497">Level All command doesn't properly resolve a resource overallocation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1498">當您有作業中有零個工作的指派時，可能無法將作業標示為完成且永遠會顯示為 99%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1498">An assignment with zero work on a task, the task may be unable to be marked complete and will always show up at 99%.</span></span>

### <a name="visio"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1499">Visio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1499">Visio</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1500">無法從 Visio 將多個圖形匯出為 SVG。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1500">Export as SVG from Visio was failing for a variety of shapes.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1501">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1501">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1502">此變更能讓使用 Word 開啟文件的效能提升。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1502">This change will lead to performance improvements in opening documents using Word.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1503">來自 Outlook 郵件中的 cid: 影像連結現在能在要求時成功中斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1503">The links of cid: images from Outlook messages can now be successfully broken when requested.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1504">我們已修正當列印到 Deskjet 印表機時，可能會導致縮放比例問題的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1504">We fixed an issue which could have caused scaling issues when printing to Deskjet printers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1505">我們已修正追蹤修訂有時候會進入無限迴圈的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1505">We fixed an issue in track changes that sometimes go into infinite loop.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1506">已修正應用程式可能在關機時懸置的各種問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1506">Fixed various issues where the app may hang on shutdown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1507">同時修正特定相關增益集當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1507">Also fixes certain add-in related crashes.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="cf135-1508">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1508">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1509">已修正不正確地將平假名和漢字中的日本新年號 "Reiwa" (令和) 識別為拼字錯誤或不合文法的運算式的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1509">Fixed an issue of incorrectly identifying the new era name “Reiwa” in Hiragana and Kanji as a misspelled or ungrammatical expression.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1510">已修正嘗試共用儲存在 SharePoint 2016 上的檔案時，導致使用者遇到「很抱歉，發生問題，無法共用」訊息的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1510">Fixed an issue which caused users to get this message "Sorry, something is preventing us from sharing this" when trying to share files stored on SharePoint 2016.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1511">已修正在 PowerPoint 共同撰寫和離線編輯的工作階段中可能會導致資料遺失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1511">Fixed issue that could cause data loss in sessions that involved both coauthoring and offline editing in PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1512">修正使用者在開啟檔案時可能會遇到的當機問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1512">This is a fix for a crash that users could hit on opening a file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1513">避免 PowerPoint 使用者嘗試進行「線上展示」時遇到錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1513">Prevents PowerPoint users from running into error when trying to Present Online.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1514">在某些情況下，同步處理引擎備份的 SharePoint 檔案可能會顯示「已儲存」但實際上未儲存任何變更，導致資料遺失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1514">In some instances, a sync-engine backed sharepoint file could show 'Saved' but not have actually saved any changes, resulting in data loss.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1515">解決使用者可能無法儲存 Word、Excel 和 PowerPoint 文件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1515">Resolved an issue where users may be unable to save Word, Excel, and PowerPoint documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1516">此問題會影響建立新檔案並在按一下 [儲存] 圖示或按 Ctrl + S 之後帶出 [另存成模型對話方塊] 選項的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1516">This issue affects users that create a new file and bring up the "Save as Dialog" option after clicking on the Save icon or pressing Ctrl + S.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1517">已修正 Win7 的效能問題，其中，於所有應用程式中從功能區插入圖案庫時，大約需要 4 秒鐘的時間才會顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1517">Fixed a perf issue on Win7 where the insert shapes gallery from the ribbon in all apps took approximately 4 seconds to appear.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1518">已修正 Backstage 的 [資訊位置] 平板未顯示協助工具資訊的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1518">Fixed a bug where accessibility information was not being displayed in the Info Place slab of the backstage.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1519">改善有關登錄完整性的 Office 更新程序的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1519">Improves reliability of the Office update process concerning registry integrity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1520">解決 Office 更新可能會非預期地從 Office CDN 而不是預期使用的來源 (例如本機或網路共用或 Configuration Manager 提供的位置) 下載檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1520">Resolved an issue where Office updates may have unexpectedly downloaded files from the Office CDN instead of the intended source, such as a local or network share, or Configuration Manager-provided location.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1521">已修正 Office 更新訊息不以預期語言顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1521">Fixed an issue where Office update messages appear in a different language than expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1522">自此以後，Office 更新訊息會正確符合 Windows 顯示語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1522">Going forward, Office update messages will correctly match the Windows display language.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1523">已解決在某些情況下，如果使用者不是系統管理員且系統帳戶沒有網路連線，將無法套用更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1523">Resolved an issue where an update would not apply in certain cases where the user is not an administrator and the System account did not have network connectivity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1524">某些情況下，Office 快速鍵可能會在更新後消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1524">In certain circumstances, Office shortcuts may disappear following an update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1525">此更新可改善發佈 Office 快速鍵時的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1525">This update improves reliability when publishing of Office shortcuts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1526">已更正可能會在計量網路上意外封鎖更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1526">Corrected an issue where updates may have been unexpectedly blocked on metered networks.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1527">修正相對期限只有在第一次設定時才會有效的 ODT 和 GPO 更新期限設定中的錯誤 (bug)。此修正可啟用後續更新的相關期限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1527">Fix to bug in ODT and GPO Update Deadline setting where relative deadline only works the first time it is set, the fix enables the relative deadline for subsequent updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1528">已改善透過恢復之前可能已中斷的下載，下載 Office 更新時的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1528">Improved reliability when downloading Office updates by resuming downloads which may have been previously interrupted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1529">已解決第三方外掛程式中與文字方塊/圖案自動調整屬性相關的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1529">Addressed issues related to Textbox/Shape Autofit property in third-party plug-ins.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1530">我們已修正大型樹狀檢視可能會導致當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1530">We fixed an issue where large tree views could result in a crash.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="cf135-1531">為了保護 Office 客戶的安全性，我們現在專門使用 SHA-2 演算法來簽署 Microsoft Office 更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cf135-1531">To protect Office customers' security, Microsoft Office updates are now signed using the SHA-2 algorithm exclusively.</span></span>
